   50 import Data.Char (ord)

   53 -- | Encode a Haskell String to a list of Word8 values, in UTF8 format.
   54 utf8Encode :: Char -> [Word8]
   55 utf8Encode = uncurry (:) . utf8Encode'
   56 
   57 utf8Encode' :: Char -> (Word8, [Word8])
   58 utf8Encode' c = case go (ord c) of
   59                   (x, xs) -> (fromIntegral x, map fromIntegral xs)
   60  where
   61   go oc
   62    | oc <= 0x7f       = ( oc
   63                         , [
   64                         ])
   65 
   66    | oc <= 0x7ff      = ( 0xc0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6)
   67                         , [0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
   68                         ])
   69 
   70    | oc <= 0xffff     = ( 0xe0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 12)
   71                         , [0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   72                         , 0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
   73                         ])
   74    | otherwise        = ( 0xf0 + (oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 18)
   75                         , [0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 12) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   76                         , 0x80 + ((oc `Data.Bits.shiftR` 6) Data.Bits..&. 0x3f)
   77                         , 0x80 + oc Data.Bits..&. 0x3f
   78                         ])
   79 
   80 #endif
   81 
   82 type Byte = Word8
   83 
   84 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
   85 -- The input type
   86 
   87 #if defined(ALEX_POSN) || defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_GSCAN)
   88 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,     -- current position,
   89                   Char,         -- previous char
   90                   [Byte],       -- pending bytes on current char
   91                   String)       -- current input string
   92 
   93 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
   94 ignorePendingBytes (p,c,_ps,s) = (p,c,[],s)
   95 
   96 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
   97 alexInputPrevChar (_p,c,_bs,_s) = c
   98 
   99 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  100 alexGetByte (p,c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(p,c,bs,s))
  101 alexGetByte (_,_,[],[]) = Nothing
  102 alexGetByte (p,_,[],(c:s))  = let p' = alexMove p c
  103                               in case utf8Encode' c of
  104                                    (b, bs) -> p' `seq`  Just (b, (p', c, bs, s))
  105 #endif
  106 
  107 #if defined (ALEX_STRICT_TEXT)
  108 type AlexInput = (Char,           -- previous char
  109                   [Byte],         -- pending bytes on current char
  110                   Data.Text.Text) -- current input string
  111 
  112 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  113 ignorePendingBytes (c,_ps,s) = (c,[],s)
  114 
  115 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  116 alexInputPrevChar (c,_bs,_s) = c
  117 
  118 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  119 alexGetByte (c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(c,bs,s))
  120 alexGetByte (_,[],s) = case Data.Text.uncons s of
  121                             Just (c, cs) ->
  122                               case utf8Encode' c of
  123                                 (b, bs) -> Just (b, (c, bs, cs))
  124                             Nothing ->
  125                               Nothing
  126 #endif
  127 
  128 #if defined (ALEX_POSN_STRICT_TEXT) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT)
  129 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,       -- current position,
  130                   Char,           -- previous char
  131                   [Byte],         -- pending bytes on current char
  132                   Data.Text.Text) -- current input string
  133 
  134 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  135 ignorePendingBytes (p,c,_ps,s) = (p,c,[],s)
  136 
  137 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  138 alexInputPrevChar (_p,c,_bs,_s) = c
  139 
  140 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  141 alexGetByte (p,c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(p,c,bs,s))
  142 alexGetByte (p,_,[],s) = case Data.Text.uncons s of
  143                             Just (c, cs) ->
  144                               let p' = alexMove p c
  145                               in case utf8Encode' c of
  146                                    (b, bs) -> p' `seq`  Just (b, (p', c, bs, cs))
  147                             Nothing ->
  148                               Nothing
  149 #endif
  150 
  151 #if defined(ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING)
  152 type AlexInput = (AlexPosn,     -- current position,
  153                   Char,         -- previous char
  154                   ByteString.ByteString,        -- current input string
  155                   Int64)           -- bytes consumed so far
  156 
  157 ignorePendingBytes :: AlexInput -> AlexInput
  158 ignorePendingBytes i = i   -- no pending bytes when lexing bytestrings
  159 
  160 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  161 alexInputPrevChar (_,c,_,_) = c
  162 
  163 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  164 alexGetByte (p,_,cs,n) =
  165     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  166         Nothing -> Nothing
  167         Just (b, cs') ->
  168             let c   = ByteString.w2c b
  169                 p'  = alexMove p c
  170                 n'  = n+1
  171             in p' `seq` cs' `seq` n' `seq` Just (b, (p', c, cs',n'))
  172 #endif
  173 
  174 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC_BYTESTRING
  175 data AlexInput = AlexInput { alexChar :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Char,      -- previous char
  176                              alexStr ::  !ByteString.ByteString,    -- current input string
  177                              alexBytePos :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Int64}  -- bytes consumed so far
  178 
  179 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  180 alexInputPrevChar = alexChar
  181 
  182 alexGetByte (AlexInput {alexStr=cs,alexBytePos=n}) =
  183     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  184         Nothing -> Nothing
  185         Just (c, rest) ->
  186             Just (c, AlexInput {
  187                 alexChar = ByteString.w2c c,
  188                 alexStr =  rest,
  189                 alexBytePos = n+1})
  190 #endif
  191 
  192 #ifdef ALEX_STRICT_BYTESTRING
  193 data AlexInput = AlexInput { alexChar :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Char,
  194                              alexStr :: {-# UNPACK #-} !ByteString.ByteString,
  195                              alexBytePos :: {-# UNPACK #-} !Int}
  196 
  197 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  198 alexInputPrevChar = alexChar
  199 
  200 alexGetByte (AlexInput {alexStr=cs,alexBytePos=n}) =
  201     case ByteString.uncons cs of
  202         Nothing -> Nothing
  203         Just (c, rest) ->
  204             Just (c, AlexInput {
  205                 alexChar = ByteString.w2c c,
  206                 alexStr =  rest,
  207                 alexBytePos = n+1})
  208 #endif

  210 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  211 -- Token positions
  212 
  213 -- `Posn' records the location of a token in the input text.  It has three
  214 -- fields: the address (number of characters preceding the token), line number
  215 -- and column of a token within the file. `start_pos' gives the position of the
  216 -- start of the file and `eof_pos' a standard encoding for the end of file.
  217 -- `move_pos' calculates the new position after traversing a given character,
  218 -- assuming the usual eight character tab stops.
  219 
  220 #if defined(ALEX_POSN) || defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_GSCAN) || defined (ALEX_POSN_STRICT_TEXT) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT)
  221 data AlexPosn = AlexPn !Int !Int !Int
  222         deriving (Eq, Show, Ord)
  223 
  224 alexStartPos :: AlexPosn
  225 alexStartPos = AlexPn 0 1 1
  226 
  227 alexMove :: AlexPosn -> Char -> AlexPosn
  228 alexMove (AlexPn a l c) '\t' = AlexPn (a+1)  l     (c+alex_tab_size-((c-1) `mod` alex_tab_size))
  229 alexMove (AlexPn a l _) '\n' = AlexPn (a+1) (l+1)   1
  230 alexMove (AlexPn a l c) _    = AlexPn (a+1)  l     (c+1)
  231 #endif
  232 
  233 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  234 -- Monad (default and with ByteString input)
  235 
  236 #if defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT)
  237 data AlexState = AlexState {
  238         alex_pos :: !AlexPosn,  -- position at current input location
  239 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  240         alex_inp :: Data.Text.Text,
  241         alex_chr :: !Char,
  242         alex_bytes :: [Byte],
  243 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT */
  244 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  245         alex_inp :: String,     -- the current input
  246         alex_chr :: !Char,      -- the character before the input
  247         alex_bytes :: [Byte],
  248 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD */
  249 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  250         alex_bpos:: !Int64,     -- bytes consumed so far
  251         alex_inp :: ByteString.ByteString,      -- the current input
  252         alex_chr :: !Char,      -- the character before the input
  253 #endif /* ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING */
  254         alex_scd :: !Int        -- the current startcode
  255 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  256       , alex_ust :: AlexUserState -- AlexUserState will be defined in the user program
  257 #endif
  258     }
  259 
  260 -- Compile with -funbox-strict-fields for best results!
  261 
  262 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  263 runAlex :: String -> Alex a -> Either String a
  264 runAlex input__ (Alex f)
  265    = case f (AlexState {alex_bytes = [],
  266                         alex_pos = alexStartPos,
  267                         alex_inp = input__,
  268                         alex_chr = '\n',
  269 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  270                         alex_ust = alexInitUserState,
  271 #endif
  272                         alex_scd = 0}) of Left msg -> Left msg
  273                                           Right ( _, a ) -> Right a
  274 #endif
  275 
  276 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  277 runAlex :: ByteString.ByteString -> Alex a -> Either String a
  278 runAlex input__ (Alex f)
  279    = case f (AlexState {alex_bpos = 0,
  280                         alex_pos = alexStartPos,
  281                         alex_inp = input__,
  282                         alex_chr = '\n',
  283 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  284                         alex_ust = alexInitUserState,
  285 #endif
  286                         alex_scd = 0}) of Left msg -> Left msg
  287                                           Right ( _, a ) -> Right a
  288 #endif
  289 
  290 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  291 runAlex :: Data.Text.Text -> Alex a -> Either String a
  292 runAlex input__ (Alex f)
  293    = case f (AlexState {alex_bytes = [],
  294                         alex_pos = alexStartPos,
  295                         alex_inp = input__,
  296                         alex_chr = '\n',
  297 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE
  298                         alex_ust = alexInitUserState,
  299 #endif
  300                         alex_scd = 0}) of Left msg -> Left msg
  301                                           Right ( _, a ) -> Right a
  302 #endif
  303 
  304 newtype Alex a = Alex { unAlex :: AlexState -> Either String (AlexState, a) }
  305 
  306 instance Functor Alex where
  307   fmap f a = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex a s of
  308                             Left msg -> Left msg
  309                             Right (s', a') -> Right (s', f a')
  310 
  311 instance Applicative Alex where
  312   pure a   = Alex $ \s -> Right (s, a)
  313   fa <*> a = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex fa s of
  314                             Left msg -> Left msg
  315                             Right (s', f) -> case unAlex a s' of
  316                                                Left msg -> Left msg
  317                                                Right (s'', b) -> Right (s'', f b)
  318 
  319 instance Monad Alex where
  320   m >>= k  = Alex $ \s -> case unAlex m s of
  321                                 Left msg -> Left msg
  322                                 Right (s',a) -> unAlex (k a) s'
  323   return = App.pure
  324 
  325 
  326 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  327 alexGetInput :: Alex AlexInput
  328 alexGetInput
  329  = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} ->
  330         Right (s, (pos,c,bs,inp__))
  331 #endif
  332 
  333 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  334 alexGetInput :: Alex AlexInput
  335 alexGetInput
  336  = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos,alex_bpos=bpos,alex_chr=c,alex_inp=inp__} ->
  337         Right (s, (pos,c,inp__,bpos))
  338 #endif
  339 
  340 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  341 alexGetInput :: Alex AlexInput
  342 alexGetInput
  343  = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} ->
  344         Right (s, (pos,c,bs,inp__))
  345 #endif
  346 
  347 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  348 alexSetInput :: AlexInput -> Alex ()
  349 alexSetInput (pos,c,bs,inp__)
  350  = Alex $ \s -> case s{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} of
  351                     state__@(AlexState{}) -> Right (state__, ())
  352 #endif
  353 
  354 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  355 alexSetInput :: AlexInput -> Alex ()
  356 alexSetInput (pos,c,inp__,bpos)
  357  = Alex $ \s -> case s{alex_pos=pos,
  358                        alex_bpos=bpos,
  359                        alex_chr=c,
  360                        alex_inp=inp__} of
  361                     state__@(AlexState{}) -> Right (state__, ())
  362 #endif
  363 
  364 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  365 alexSetInput :: AlexInput -> Alex ()
  366 alexSetInput (pos,c,bs,inp__)
  367  = Alex $ \s -> case s{alex_pos=pos,alex_chr=c,alex_bytes=bs,alex_inp=inp__} of
  368                     state__@(AlexState{}) -> Right (state__, ())
  369 #endif
  370 
  371 alexError :: String -> Alex a
  372 alexError message = Alex $ const $ Left message
  373 
  374 alexGetStartCode :: Alex Int
  375 alexGetStartCode = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_scd=sc} -> Right (s, sc)
  376 
  377 alexSetStartCode :: Int -> Alex ()
  378 alexSetStartCode sc = Alex $ \s -> Right (s{alex_scd=sc}, ())
  379 
  380 #if defined(ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE)
  381 alexGetUserState :: Alex AlexUserState
  382 alexGetUserState = Alex $ \s@AlexState{alex_ust=ust} -> Right (s,ust)
  383 
  384 alexSetUserState :: AlexUserState -> Alex ()
  385 alexSetUserState ss = Alex $ \s -> Right (s{alex_ust=ss}, ())
  386 #endif /* defined(ALEX_MONAD_USER_STATE) */
  387 
  388 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  389 alexMonadScan = do
  390   inp__ <- alexGetInput
  391   sc <- alexGetStartCode
  392   case alexScan inp__ sc of
  393     AlexEOF -> alexEOF
  394     AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> alexError $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  395     AlexSkip  inp__' _len -> do
  396         alexSetInput inp__'
  397         alexMonadScan
  398     AlexToken inp__' len action -> do
  399         alexSetInput inp__'
  400         action (ignorePendingBytes inp__) len
  401 #endif
  402 
  403 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  404 alexMonadScan = do
  405   inp__@(_,_,_,n) <- alexGetInput
  406   sc <- alexGetStartCode
  407   case alexScan inp__ sc of
  408     AlexEOF -> alexEOF
  409     AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> alexError $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  410     AlexSkip  inp__' _len -> do
  411         alexSetInput inp__'
  412         alexMonadScan
  413     AlexToken inp__'@(_,_,_,n') _ action -> let len = n'-n in do
  414         alexSetInput inp__'
  415         action (ignorePendingBytes inp__) len
  416 #endif
  417 
  418 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  419 alexMonadScan = do
  420   inp__ <- alexGetInput
  421   sc <- alexGetStartCode
  422   case alexScan inp__ sc of
  423     AlexEOF -> alexEOF
  424     AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> alexError $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  425     AlexSkip  inp__' _len -> do
  426         alexSetInput inp__'
  427         alexMonadScan
  428     AlexToken inp__' len action -> do
  429         alexSetInput inp__'
  430         action (ignorePendingBytes inp__) len
  431 #endif
  432 
  433 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  434 -- Useful token actions
  435 
  436 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  437 type AlexAction result = AlexInput -> Int -> Alex result
  438 #endif
  439 
  440 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  441 type AlexAction result = AlexInput -> Int64 -> Alex result
  442 #endif
  443 
  444 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  445 type AlexAction result = AlexInput -> Int -> Alex result
  446 #endif
  447 
  448 -- just ignore this token and scan another one
  449 -- skip :: AlexAction result
  450 skip _input _len = alexMonadScan
  451 
  452 -- ignore this token, but set the start code to a new value
  453 -- begin :: Int -> AlexAction result
  454 begin code _input _len = do alexSetStartCode code; alexMonadScan
  455 
  456 -- perform an action for this token, and set the start code to a new value
  457 andBegin :: AlexAction result -> Int -> AlexAction result
  458 (action `andBegin` code) input__ len = do
  459   alexSetStartCode code
  460   action input__ len
  461 
  462 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD
  463 token :: (AlexInput -> Int -> token) -> AlexAction token
  464 token t input__ len = return (t input__ len)
  465 #endif
  466 
  467 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING
  468 token :: (AlexInput -> Int64 -> token) -> AlexAction token
  469 token t input__ len = return (t input__ len)
  470 #endif
  471 
  472 #ifdef ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT
  473 token :: (AlexInput -> Int -> token) -> AlexAction token
  474 token t input__ len = return (t input__ len)
  475 #endif
  476 
  477 #endif /* defined(ALEX_MONAD) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_BYTESTRING) || defined(ALEX_MONAD_STRICT_TEXT) */

  479 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  480 -- Basic wrapper
  481 
  482 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC
  483 type AlexInput = (Char,[Byte],String)
  484 
  485 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  486 alexInputPrevChar (c,_,_) = c
  487 
  488 -- alexScanTokens :: String -> [token]
  489 alexScanTokens str = go ('\n',[],str)
  490   where go inp__@(_,_bs,s) =
  491           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  492                 AlexEOF -> []
  493                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  494                 AlexSkip  inp__' _ln     -> go inp__'
  495                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act (take len s) : go inp__'
  496 
  497 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Byte,AlexInput)
  498 alexGetByte (c,(b:bs),s) = Just (b,(c,bs,s))
  499 alexGetByte (_,[],[])    = Nothing
  500 alexGetByte (_,[],(c:s)) = case utf8Encode' c of
  501                              (b, bs) -> Just (b, (c, bs, s))
  502 #endif
  503 
  504 
  505 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  506 -- Basic wrapper, ByteString version
  507 
  508 #ifdef ALEX_BASIC_BYTESTRING
  509 
  510 -- alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  511 alexScanTokens str = go (AlexInput '\n' str 0)
  512   where go inp__ =
  513           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  514                 AlexEOF -> []
  515                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  516                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  517                 AlexToken inp__' _ act ->
  518                   let len = alexBytePos inp__' - alexBytePos inp__ in
  519                   act (ByteString.take len (alexStr inp__)) : go inp__'
  520 
  521 #endif
  522 
  523 #ifdef ALEX_STRICT_BYTESTRING
  524 
  525 -- alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  526 alexScanTokens str = go (AlexInput '\n' str 0)
  527   where go inp__ =
  528           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  529                 AlexEOF -> []
  530                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  531                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  532                 AlexToken inp__' _ act ->
  533                   let len = alexBytePos inp__' - alexBytePos inp__ in
  534                   act (ByteString.take len (alexStr inp__)) : go inp__'
  535 
  536 #endif
  537 
  538 #ifdef ALEX_STRICT_TEXT
  539 -- alexScanTokens :: Data.Text.Text -> [token]
  540 alexScanTokens str = go ('\n',[],str)
  541   where go inp__@(_,_bs,s) =
  542           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  543                 AlexEOF -> []
  544                 AlexError _ -> error "lexical error"
  545                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  546                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act (Data.Text.take len s) : go inp__'
  547 #endif
  548 
  549 #ifdef ALEX_POSN_STRICT_TEXT
  550 -- alexScanTokens :: Data.Text.Text -> [token]
  551 alexScanTokens str = go (alexStartPos,'\n',[],str)
  552   where go inp__@(pos,_,_bs,s) =
  553           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  554                 AlexEOF -> []
  555                 AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  556                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len  -> go inp__'
  557                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act pos (Data.Text.take len s) : go inp__'
  558 #endif
  559 
  560 
  561 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  562 -- Posn wrapper
  563 
  564 -- Adds text positions to the basic model.
  565 
  566 #ifdef ALEX_POSN
  567 --alexScanTokens :: String -> [token]
  568 alexScanTokens str0 = go (alexStartPos,'\n',[],str0)
  569   where go inp__@(pos,_,_,str) =
  570           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  571                 AlexEOF -> []
  572                 AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  573                 AlexSkip  inp__' _ln     -> go inp__'
  574                 AlexToken inp__' len act -> act pos (take len str) : go inp__'
  575 #endif
  576 
  577 
  578 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  579 -- Posn wrapper, ByteString version
  580 
  581 #ifdef ALEX_POSN_BYTESTRING
  582 --alexScanTokens :: ByteString.ByteString -> [token]
  583 alexScanTokens str0 = go (alexStartPos,'\n',str0,0)
  584   where go inp__@(pos,_,str,n) =
  585           case alexScan inp__ 0 of
  586                 AlexEOF -> []
  587                 AlexError ((AlexPn _ line column),_,_,_) -> error $ "lexical error at line " ++ (show line) ++ ", column " ++ (show column)
  588                 AlexSkip  inp__' _len       -> go inp__'
  589                 AlexToken inp__'@(_,_,_,n') _ act ->
  590                   act pos (ByteString.take (n'-n) str) : go inp__'
  591 #endif
  592 
  593 
  594 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  595 -- GScan wrapper
  596 
  597 -- For compatibility with previous versions of Alex, and because we can.
  598 
  599 #ifdef ALEX_GSCAN
  600 alexGScan stop__ state__ inp__ =
  601   alex_gscan stop__ alexStartPos '\n' [] inp__ (0,state__)
  602 
  603 alex_gscan stop__ p c bs inp__ (sc,state__) =
  604   case alexScan (p,c,bs,inp__) sc of
  605         AlexEOF     -> stop__ p c inp__ (sc,state__)
  606         AlexError _ -> stop__ p c inp__ (sc,state__)
  607         AlexSkip (p',c',bs',inp__') _len ->
  608           alex_gscan stop__ p' c' bs' inp__' (sc,state__)
  609         AlexToken (p',c',bs',inp__') len k ->
  610            k p c inp__ len (\scs -> alex_gscan stop__ p' c' bs' inp__' scs)                  (sc,state__)
  611 #endif
  612 alex_tab_size :: Int
  613 alex_tab_size = 8
  614 alex_base :: AlexAddr
  615 alex_base = AlexA#

 1102 #define ALEX_GHC 1
 1103 #define ALEX_NOPRED 1
 1104 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1105 -- ALEX TEMPLATE
 1106 --
 1107 -- This code is in the PUBLIC DOMAIN; you may copy it freely and use
 1108 -- it for any purpose whatsoever.
 1109 
 1110 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1111 -- INTERNALS and main scanner engine
 1112 
 1113 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
 1114 #  define ILIT(n) n#
 1115 #  define IBOX(n) (I# (n))
 1116 #  define FAST_INT Int#
 1117 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
 1118 #  if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
 1119 #    define GTE(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n >=# m))
 1120 #    define EQ(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n ==# m))
 1121 #  else
 1122 #    define GTE(n,m) (n >=# m)
 1123 #    define EQ(n,m) (n ==# m)
 1124 #  endif
 1125 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n +# m)
 1126 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n -# m)
 1127 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n *# m)
 1128 #  define NEGATE(n) (negateInt# (n))
 1129 #  define IF_GHC(x) (x)
 1130 #else
 1131 #  define ILIT(n) (n)
 1132 #  define IBOX(n) (n)
 1133 #  define FAST_INT Int
 1134 #  define GTE(n,m) (n >= m)
 1135 #  define EQ(n,m) (n == m)
 1136 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n + m)
 1137 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n - m)
 1138 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n * m)
 1139 #  define NEGATE(n) (negate (n))
 1140 #  define IF_GHC(x)
 1141 #endif
 1142 
 1143 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
 1144 data AlexAddr = AlexA# Addr#
 1145 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
 1146 
 1147 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt16OffAddr #-}
 1148 alexIndexInt16OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
 1149 alexIndexInt16OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
 1150 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
 1151   narrow16Int# i
 1152   where
 1153         i    = word2Int# ((high `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` low)
 1154         high = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
 1155         low  = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
 1156         off' = off *# 2#
 1157 #else
 1158 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
 1159   GHC.Exts.int16ToInt#
 1160 #endif
 1161     (indexInt16OffAddr# arr off)
 1162 #endif
 1163 #else
 1164 alexIndexInt16OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
 1165 #endif
 1166 
 1167 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
 1168 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt32OffAddr #-}
 1169 alexIndexInt32OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
 1170 alexIndexInt32OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
 1171 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
 1172   narrow32Int# i
 1173   where
 1174    i    = word2Int# ((b3 `uncheckedShiftL#` 24#) `or#`
 1175                      (b2 `uncheckedShiftL#` 16#) `or#`
 1176                      (b1 `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` b0)
 1177    b3   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 3#)))
 1178    b2   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 2#)))
 1179    b1   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
 1180    b0   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
 1181    off' = off *# 4#
 1182 #else
 1183 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
 1184   GHC.Exts.int32ToInt#
 1185 #endif
 1186     (indexInt32OffAddr# arr off)
 1187 #endif
 1188 #else
 1189 alexIndexInt32OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
 1190 #endif
 1191 
 1192 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
 1193 -- GHC >= 503, unsafeAt is available from Data.Array.Base.
 1194 quickIndex = unsafeAt
 1195 #else
 1196 quickIndex = (Data.Array.!)
 1197 #endif
 1198 
 1199 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1200 -- Main lexing routines
 1201 
 1202 data AlexReturn a
 1203   = AlexEOF
 1204   | AlexError  !AlexInput
 1205   | AlexSkip   !AlexInput !Int
 1206   | AlexToken  !AlexInput !Int a
 1207 
 1208 -- alexScan :: AlexInput -> StartCode -> AlexReturn a
 1209 alexScan input__ IBOX(sc)
 1210   = alexScanUser undefined input__ IBOX(sc)
 1211 
 1212 alexScanUser user__ input__ IBOX(sc)
 1213   = case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
 1214   (AlexNone, input__') ->
 1215     case alexGetByte input__ of
 1216       Nothing ->
 1217 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1218                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("End of input.") $
 1219 #endif
 1220                                    AlexEOF
 1221       Just _ ->
 1222 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1223                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("Error.") $
 1224 #endif
 1225                                    AlexError input__'
 1226 
 1227   (AlexLastSkip input__'' len, _) ->
 1228 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1229     Debug.Trace.trace ("Skipping.") $
 1230 #endif
 1231     AlexSkip input__'' len
 1232 
 1233   (AlexLastAcc k input__''' len, _) ->
 1234 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1235     Debug.Trace.trace ("Accept.") $
 1236 #endif
 1237     AlexToken input__''' len ((Data.Array.!) alex_actions k)
 1238 
 1239 
 1240 -- Push the input through the DFA, remembering the most recent accepting
 1241 -- state it encountered.
 1242 
 1243 alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input len input__ s last_acc =
 1244   input__ `seq` -- strict in the input
 1245   let
 1246   new_acc = (check_accs (alex_accept `quickIndex` IBOX(s)))
 1247   in
 1248   new_acc `seq`
 1249   case alexGetByte input__ of
 1250      Nothing -> (new_acc, input__)
 1251      Just (c, new_input) ->
 1252 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
 1253       Debug.Trace.trace ("State: " ++ show IBOX(s) ++ ", char: " ++ show c ++ " " ++ (show . chr . fromIntegral) c) $
 1254 #endif
 1255       case fromIntegral c of { IBOX(ord_c) ->
 1256         let
 1257                 base   = alexIndexInt32OffAddr alex_base s
 1258                 offset = PLUS(base,ord_c)
 1259 
 1260                 new_s = if GTE(offset,ILIT(0))
 1261                           && let check  = alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_check offset
 1262                              in  EQ(check,ord_c)
 1263                           then alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_table offset
 1264                           else alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_deflt s
 1265         in
 1266         case new_s of
 1267             ILIT(-1) -> (new_acc, input__)
 1268                 -- on an error, we want to keep the input *before* the
 1269                 -- character that failed, not after.
 1270             _ -> alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input
 1271 #ifdef ALEX_LATIN1
 1272                    PLUS(len,ILIT(1))
 1273                    -- issue 119: in the latin1 encoding, *each* byte is one character
 1274 #else
 1275                    (if c < 0x80 || c >= 0xC0 then PLUS(len,ILIT(1)) else len)
 1276                    -- note that the length is increased ONLY if this is the 1st byte in a char encoding)
 1277 #endif
 1278                    new_input new_s new_acc
 1279       }
 1280   where
 1281         check_accs (AlexAccNone) = last_acc
 1282         check_accs (AlexAcc a  ) = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
 1283         check_accs (AlexAccSkip) = AlexLastSkip  input__ IBOX(len)
 1284 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
 1285         check_accs (AlexAccPred a predx rest)
 1286            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
 1287            = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
 1288            | otherwise
 1289            = check_accs rest
 1290         check_accs (AlexAccSkipPred predx rest)
 1291            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
 1292            = AlexLastSkip input__ IBOX(len)
 1293            | otherwise
 1294            = check_accs rest
 1295 #endif
 1296 
 1297 data AlexLastAcc
 1298   = AlexNone
 1299   | AlexLastAcc !Int !AlexInput !Int
 1300   | AlexLastSkip     !AlexInput !Int
 1301 
 1302 data AlexAcc user
 1303   = AlexAccNone
 1304   | AlexAcc Int
 1305   | AlexAccSkip
 1306 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
 1307   | AlexAccPred Int (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
 1308   | AlexAccSkipPred (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
 1309 
 1310 type AlexAccPred user = user -> AlexInput -> Int -> AlexInput -> Bool
 1311 
 1312 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1313 -- Predicates on a rule
 1314 
 1315 alexAndPred p1 p2 user__ in1 len in2
 1316   = p1 user__ in1 len in2 && p2 user__ in1 len in2
 1317 
 1318 --alexPrevCharIsPred :: Char -> AlexAccPred _
 1319 alexPrevCharIs c _ input__ _ _ = c == alexInputPrevChar input__
 1320 
 1321 alexPrevCharMatches f _ input__ _ _ = f (alexInputPrevChar input__)
 1322 
 1323 --alexPrevCharIsOneOfPred :: Array Char Bool -> AlexAccPred _
 1324 alexPrevCharIsOneOf arr _ input__ _ _ = arr Data.Array.! alexInputPrevChar input__
 1325 
 1326 --alexRightContext :: Int -> AlexAccPred _
 1327 alexRightContext IBOX(sc) user__ _ _ input__ =
 1328      case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
 1329           (AlexNone, _) -> False
 1330           _ -> True
 1331         -- TODO: there's no need to find the longest
 1332         -- match when checking the right context, just
 1333         -- the first match will do.
 1334 #endif
 1335 {-# LINE 84 "heapster/src/Heapster/Lexer.x" #-}
 1336 -- | Convert alex-specific position type to public interface.
 1337 mkPos :: AlexPosn -> Pos
 1338 mkPos (AlexPn x y z) = Pos x y z
 1339 
 1340 -- | Helper for building a 'Located' 'Token'
 1341 token :: (String -> Token) -> AlexPosn -> String -> Located Token
 1342 token tok p str = Located (mkPos p) (tok str)
 1343 
 1344 -- | Helper for building a 'Located' 'Token' with no argument
 1345 token_ :: Token -> AlexPosn -> String -> Located Token
 1346 token_ tok p _ = Located (mkPos p) tok
 1347

 1349 -- reported inline with the 'TError' token.
 1350 lexer ::
 1351   String                {- ^ input text                 -} ->
 1352   [Located Token]       {- ^ token stream               -}
 1353 lexer = alexScanTokens
